It is not too far from the city and is relatively cheap. It is not close to the subway but not too far away, and the transportation is relatively convenient.
The interior of the room is relatively high-end, and the bathroom is also separated from the bathtub and shower, which is a good point. However, the interior space of the room is small. I think as a high-end hotel, the interior space of its guest rooms should be larger than this. The takeaway can be delivered directly to the door, which is very good (I can deliver the takeaway at one or two o'clock in the morning).
There is no big problem with hygiene, it is relatively neat and clean. But there is a problem with this air conditioner. I donâ€™t know if it is the case with air conditioners in the south. I obviously adjusted it to 5 degrees but it is still not too cold.
Another problem is the guest room TV. The customization level of this guest room TV is too low. Except for the boot interface, the rest is the same as ordinary smart TVs, that is, almost any function must be paid, and even CCTV1 can only be tried for five minutes.
